           <div class="finance-tab-content-head row">
            <div class="finance-tab-content-head-col-1 clr">
             <h2>
              <a href="https://finans.mynet.com/borsa/endeks/xu100-bist-100/" title="Mynet Finans">
               BIST 100
              </a>
             </h2>
             <span>
